<div><h2 id="class-" style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin-right: 0px; margin-bottom: 16px; margin-left: 0px; padding: 0px 0px 0.3em; top: -900em; left: -900em; box-sizing: border-box; border-bottom: 1px solid rgb(238, 238, 238); line-height: 1.25; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Roboto, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif, &quot;Apple Color Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Symbol&quot;; margin-top: 0px !important;">Class基本语法</h2><h3 id="-" style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin: 24px 0px 16px; padding: 0px; font-size: 1.25em; box-sizing: border-box; line-height: 1.25; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Roboto, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif, &quot;Apple Color Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Symbol&quot;;">概述</h3><p style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin: 0px 0px 16px; padding: 0px; box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Roboto, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif, &quot;Apple Color Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Symbol&quot;;">JavaScript语言的传统方法是通过构造函数，定义并生成新对象。下面是一个例子。</p><pre style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 16px; padding: 16px; box-sizing: border-box; font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-stretch: normal; font-size: 12px; line-height: 1.45; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; word-wrap: normal; overflow: auto; background-color: rgb(247, 247, 247); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51);"><code class="lang-javascript" style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0px; margin: 0px; background: 0px 0px transparent; border-radius: 3px; word-break: normal; white-space: pre; border: 0px; display: inline; overflow: visible; line-height: inherit; word-wrap: normal; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">function Point(x, y) {
  this.x = x;
  this.y = y;
}

Point.prototype.toString = function () {
  return '(' + this.x + ', ' + this.y + ')';
};

var p = new Point(1, 2);
</code></pre><p style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin: 0px 0px 16px; padding: 0px; box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Roboto, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif, &quot;Apple Color Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Symbol&quot;;">上面这种写法跟传统的面向对象语言（比如C++和Java）差异很大，很容易让新学习这门语言的程序员感到困惑。</p><p style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin: 0px 0px 16px; padding: 0px; box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Roboto, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif, &quot;Apple Color Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Symbol&quot;;">ES6提供了更接近传统语言的写法，引入了Class（类）这个概念，作为对象的模板。通过<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">class</code>关键字，可以定义类。基本上，ES6的<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">class</code>可以看作只是一个语法糖，它的绝大部分功能，ES5都可以做到，新的<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">class</code>写法只是让对象原型的写法更加清晰、更像面向对象编程的语法而已。上面的代码用ES6的“类”改写，就是下面这样。</p><pre style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 16px; padding: 16px; box-sizing: border-box; font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-stretch: normal; font-size: 12px; line-height: 1.45; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; word-wrap: normal; overflow: auto; background-color: rgb(247, 247, 247); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51);"><code class="lang-javascript" style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0px; margin: 0px; background: 0px 0px transparent; border-radius: 3px; word-break: normal; white-space: pre; border: 0px; display: inline; overflow: visible; line-height: inherit; word-wrap: normal; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">//定义类
class Point {
  constructor(x, y) {
    this.x = x;
    this.y = y;
  }

  toString() {
    return '(' + this.x + ', ' + this.y + ')';
  }
}
</code></pre><p style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin: 0px 0px 16px; padding: 0px; box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Roboto, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif, &quot;Apple Color Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Symbol&quot;;">上面代码定义了一个“类”，可以看到里面有一个<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">constructor</code>方法，这就是构造方法，而<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">this</code>关键字则代表实例对象。也就是说，ES5的构造函数<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">Point</code>，对应ES6的<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">Point</code>类的构造方法。</p><p style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin: 0px 0px 16px; padding: 0px; box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Roboto, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif, &quot;Apple Color Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Symbol&quot;;"><code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">Point</code>类除了构造方法，还定义了一个<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">toString</code>方法。注意，定义“类”的方法的时候，前面不需要加上<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">function</code>这个关键字，直接把函数定义放进去了就可以了。另外，方法之间不需要逗号分隔，加了会报错。</p><p style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin: 0px 0px 16px; padding: 0px; box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Roboto, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif, &quot;Apple Color Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Symbol&quot;;">ES6的类，完全可以看作构造函数的另一种写法。</p><pre style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 16px; padding: 16px; box-sizing: border-box; font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-stretch: normal; font-size: 12px; line-height: 1.45; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; word-wrap: normal; overflow: auto; background-color: rgb(247, 247, 247); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51);"><code class="lang-javascript" style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0px; margin: 0px; background: 0px 0px transparent; border-radius: 3px; word-break: normal; white-space: pre; border: 0px; display: inline; overflow: visible; line-height: inherit; word-wrap: normal; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">class Point {
  // ...
}

typeof Point // "function"
Point === Point.prototype.constructor // true
</code></pre><p style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin: 0px 0px 16px; padding: 0px; box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Roboto, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif, &quot;Apple Color Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Symbol&quot;;">上面代码表明，类的数据类型就是函数，类本身就指向构造函数。</p><p style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin: 0px 0px 16px; padding: 0px; box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Roboto, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif, &quot;Apple Color Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Symbol&quot;;">使用的时候，也是直接对类使用<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">new</code>命令，跟构造函数的用法完全一致。</p><pre style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 16px; padding: 16px; box-sizing: border-box; font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-stretch: normal; font-size: 12px; line-height: 1.45; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; word-wrap: normal; overflow: auto; background-color: rgb(247, 247, 247); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51);"><code class="lang-javascript" style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0px; margin: 0px; background: 0px 0px transparent; border-radius: 3px; word-break: normal; white-space: pre; border: 0px; display: inline; overflow: visible; line-height: inherit; word-wrap: normal; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">class Bar {
  doStuff() {
    console.log('stuff');
  }
}

var b = new Bar();
b.doStuff() // "stuff"
</code></pre><p style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin: 0px 0px 16px; padding: 0px; box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Roboto, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif, &quot;Apple Color Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Symbol&quot;;">构造函数的<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">prototype</code>属性，在ES6的“类”上面继续存在。事实上，类的所有方法都定义在类的<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">prototype</code>属性上面。</p><pre style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 16px; padding: 16px; box-sizing: border-box; font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-stretch: normal; font-size: 12px; line-height: 1.45; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; word-wrap: normal; overflow: auto; background-color: rgb(247, 247, 247); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51);"><code class="lang-javascript" style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0px; margin: 0px; background: 0px 0px transparent; border-radius: 3px; word-break: normal; white-space: pre; border: 0px; display: inline; overflow: visible; line-height: inherit; word-wrap: normal; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">class Point {
  constructor(){
    // ...
  }

  toString(){
    // ...
  }

  toValue(){
    // ...
  }
}

// 等同于

Point.prototype = {
  toString(){},
  toValue(){}
};
</code></pre><p style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin: 0px 0px 16px; padding: 0px; box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Roboto, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif, &quot;Apple Color Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Symbol&quot;;">在类的实例上面调用方法，其实就是调用原型上的方法。</p><pre style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 16px; padding: 16px; box-sizing: border-box; font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-stretch: normal; font-size: 12px; line-height: 1.45; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; word-wrap: normal; overflow: auto; background-color: rgb(247, 247, 247); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51);"><code class="lang-javascript" style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0px; margin: 0px; background: 0px 0px transparent; border-radius: 3px; word-break: normal; white-space: pre; border: 0px; display: inline; overflow: visible; line-height: inherit; word-wrap: normal; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">class B {}
let b = new B();

b.constructor === B.prototype.constructor // true
</code></pre><p style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin: 0px 0px 16px; padding: 0px; box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Roboto, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif, &quot;Apple Color Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Symbol&quot;;">上面代码中，<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">b</code>是B类的实例，它的<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">constructor</code>方法就是B类原型的<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">constructor</code>方法。</p><p style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin: 0px 0px 16px; padding: 0px; box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Roboto, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif, &quot;Apple Color Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Symbol&quot;;">由于类的方法都定义在<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">prototype</code>对象上面，所以类的新方法可以添加在<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">prototype</code>对象上面。<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">Object.assign</code>方法可以很方便地一次向类添加多个方法。</p><pre style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 16px; padding: 16px; box-sizing: border-box; font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-stretch: normal; font-size: 12px; line-height: 1.45; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; word-wrap: normal; overflow: auto; background-color: rgb(247, 247, 247); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51);"><code class="lang-javascript" style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0px; margin: 0px; background: 0px 0px transparent; border-radius: 3px; word-break: normal; white-space: pre; border: 0px; display: inline; overflow: visible; line-height: inherit; word-wrap: normal; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">class Point {
  constructor(){
    // ...
  }
}

Object.assign(Point.prototype, {
  toString(){},
  toValue(){}
});
</code></pre><p style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin: 0px 0px 16px; padding: 0px; box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Roboto, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif, &quot;Apple Color Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Symbol&quot;;"><code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">prototype</code>对象的<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">constructor</code>属性，直接指向“类”的本身，这与ES5的行为是一致的。</p><pre style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 16px; padding: 16px; box-sizing: border-box; font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-stretch: normal; font-size: 12px; line-height: 1.45; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; word-wrap: normal; overflow: auto; background-color: rgb(247, 247, 247); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51);"><code class="lang-javascript" style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0px; margin: 0px; background: 0px 0px transparent; border-radius: 3px; word-break: normal; white-space: pre; border: 0px; display: inline; overflow: visible; line-height: inherit; word-wrap: normal; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">Point.prototype.constructor === Point // true
</code></pre><p style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin: 0px 0px 16px; padding: 0px; box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Roboto, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif, &quot;Apple Color Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Symbol&quot;;">另外，类的内部所有定义的方法，都是不可枚举的（non-enumerable）。</p><pre style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 16px; padding: 16px; box-sizing: border-box; font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-stretch: normal; font-size: 12px; line-height: 1.45; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; word-wrap: normal; overflow: auto; background-color: rgb(247, 247, 247); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51);"><code class="lang-javascript" style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0px; margin: 0px; background: 0px 0px transparent; border-radius: 3px; word-break: normal; white-space: pre; border: 0px; display: inline; overflow: visible; line-height: inherit; word-wrap: normal; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">class Point {
  constructor(x, y) {
    // ...
  }

  toString() {
    // ...
  }
}

Object.keys(Point.prototype)
// []
Object.getOwnPropertyNames(Point.prototype)
// ["constructor","toString"]
</code></pre><p style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin: 0px 0px 16px; padding: 0px; box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Roboto, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif, &quot;Apple Color Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Symbol&quot;;">上面代码中，<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">toString</code>方法是<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">Point</code>类内部定义的方法，它是不可枚举的。这一点与ES5的行为不一致。</p><pre style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 16px; padding: 16px; box-sizing: border-box; font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-stretch: normal; font-size: 12px; line-height: 1.45; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; word-wrap: normal; overflow: auto; background-color: rgb(247, 247, 247); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51);"><code class="lang-javascript" style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0px; margin: 0px; background: 0px 0px transparent; border-radius: 3px; word-break: normal; white-space: pre; border: 0px; display: inline; overflow: visible; line-height: inherit; word-wrap: normal; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">var Point = function (x, y) {
  // ...
};

Point.prototype.toString = function() {
  // ...
};

Object.keys(Point.prototype)
// ["toString"]
Object.getOwnPropertyNames(Point.prototype)
// ["constructor","toString"]
</code></pre><p style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin: 0px 0px 16px; padding: 0px; box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Roboto, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif, &quot;Apple Color Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Symbol&quot;;">上面代码采用ES5的写法，<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">toString</code>方法就是可枚举的。</p><p style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin: 0px 0px 16px; padding: 0px; box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Roboto, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif, &quot;Apple Color Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Symbol&quot;;">类的属性名，可以采用表达式。</p><pre style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 16px; padding: 16px; box-sizing: border-box; font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-stretch: normal; font-size: 12px; line-height: 1.45; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; word-wrap: normal; overflow: auto; background-color: rgb(247, 247, 247); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51);"><code class="lang-javascript" style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0px; margin: 0px; background: 0px 0px transparent; border-radius: 3px; word-break: normal; white-space: pre; border: 0px; display: inline; overflow: visible; line-height: inherit; word-wrap: normal; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">let methodName = "getArea";
class Square{
  constructor(length) {
    // ...
  }

  [methodName]() {
    // ...
  }
}
</code></pre><p style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin: 0px 0px 16px; padding: 0px; box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Roboto, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif, &quot;Apple Color Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Symbol&quot;;">上面代码中，<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">Square</code>类的方法名<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">getArea</code>，是从表达式得到的。</p><h3 id="constructor-" style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin: 24px 0px 16px; padding: 0px; font-size: 1.25em; box-sizing: border-box; line-height: 1.25; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Roboto, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif, &quot;Apple Color Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Symbol&quot;;">constructor方法</h3><p style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin: 0px 0px 16px; padding: 0px; box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Roboto, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif, &quot;Apple Color Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Symbol&quot;;"><code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">constructor</code>方法是类的默认方法，通过<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">new</code>命令生成对象实例时，自动调用该方法。一个类必须有<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">constructor</code>方法，如果没有显式定义，一个空的<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">constructor</code>方法会被默认添加。</p><pre style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 16px; padding: 16px; box-sizing: border-box; font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-stretch: normal; font-size: 12px; line-height: 1.45; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; word-wrap: normal; overflow: auto; background-color: rgb(247, 247, 247); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51);"><code class="lang-javascript" style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0px; margin: 0px; background: 0px 0px transparent; border-radius: 3px; word-break: normal; white-space: pre; border: 0px; display: inline; overflow: visible; line-height: inherit; word-wrap: normal; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">constructor() {}
</code></pre><p style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin: 0px 0px 16px; padding: 0px; box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Roboto, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif, &quot;Apple Color Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Symbol&quot;;"><code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">constructor</code>方法默认返回实例对象（即<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">this</code>），完全可以指定返回另外一个对象。</p><pre style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 16px; padding: 16px; box-sizing: border-box; font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-stretch: normal; font-size: 12px; line-height: 1.45; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; word-wrap: normal; overflow: auto; background-color: rgb(247, 247, 247); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51);"><code class="lang-javascript" style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0px; margin: 0px; background: 0px 0px transparent; border-radius: 3px; word-break: normal; white-space: pre; border: 0px; display: inline; overflow: visible; line-height: inherit; word-wrap: normal; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">class Foo {
  constructor() {
    return Object.create(null);
  }
}

new Foo() instanceof Foo
// false
</code></pre><p style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin: 0px 0px 16px; padding: 0px; box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Roboto, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif, &quot;Apple Color Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Symbol&quot;;">上面代码中，<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">constructor</code>函数返回一个全新的对象，结果导致实例对象不是<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">Foo</code>类的实例。</p><p style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin: 0px 0px 16px; padding: 0px; box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Roboto, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif, &quot;Apple Color Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Symbol&quot;;">类的构造函数，不使用<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">new</code>是没法调用的，会报错。这是它跟普通构造函数的一个主要区别，后者不用<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">new</code>也可以执行。</p><pre style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 16px; padding: 16px; box-sizing: border-box; font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-stretch: normal; font-size: 12px; line-height: 1.45; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; word-wrap: normal; overflow: auto; background-color: rgb(247, 247, 247); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51);"><code class="lang-javascript" style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0px; margin: 0px; background: 0px 0px transparent; border-radius: 3px; word-break: normal; white-space: pre; border: 0px; display: inline; overflow: visible; line-height: inherit; word-wrap: normal; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">class Foo {
  constructor() {
    return Object.create(null);
  }
}

Foo()
// TypeError: Class constructor Foo cannot be invoked without 'new'
</code></pre><h3 id="-" style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin: 24px 0px 16px; padding: 0px; font-size: 1.25em; box-sizing: border-box; line-height: 1.25; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Roboto, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif, &quot;Apple Color Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Symbol&quot;;">类的实例对象</h3><p style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin: 0px 0px 16px; padding: 0px; box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Roboto, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif, &quot;Apple Color Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Symbol&quot;;">生成类的实例对象的写法，与ES5完全一样，也是使用<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">new</code>命令。如果忘记加上<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">new</code>，像函数那样调用<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">Class</code>，将会报错。</p><pre style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 16px; padding: 16px; box-sizing: border-box; font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-stretch: normal; font-size: 12px; line-height: 1.45; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; word-wrap: normal; overflow: auto; background-color: rgb(247, 247, 247); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51);"><code class="lang-javascript" style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0px; margin: 0px; background: 0px 0px transparent; border-radius: 3px; word-break: normal; white-space: pre; border: 0px; display: inline; overflow: visible; line-height: inherit; word-wrap: normal; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">// 报错
var point = Point(2, 3);

// 正确
var point = new Point(2, 3);
</code></pre><p style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin: 0px 0px 16px; padding: 0px; box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Roboto, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif, &quot;Apple Color Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Symbol&quot;;">与ES5一样，实例的属性除非显式定义在其本身（即定义在<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">this</code>对象上），否则都是定义在原型上（即定义在<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">class</code>上）。</p><pre style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 16px; padding: 16px; box-sizing: border-box; font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-stretch: normal; font-size: 12px; line-height: 1.45; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; word-wrap: normal; overflow: auto; background-color: rgb(247, 247, 247); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51);"><code class="lang-javascript" style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0px; margin: 0px; background: 0px 0px transparent; border-radius: 3px; word-break: normal; white-space: pre; border: 0px; display: inline; overflow: visible; line-height: inherit; word-wrap: normal; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">//定义类
class Point {

  constructor(x, y) {
    this.x = x;
    this.y = y;
  }

  toString() {
    return '(' + this.x + ', ' + this.y + ')';
  }

}

var point = new Point(2, 3);

point.toString() // (2, 3)

point.hasOwnProperty('x') // true
point.hasOwnProperty('y') // true
point.hasOwnProperty('toString') // false
point.__proto__.hasOwnProperty('toString') // true
</code></pre><p style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin: 0px 0px 16px; padding: 0px; box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Roboto, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif, &quot;Apple Color Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Symbol&quot;;">上面代码中，<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">x</code>和<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">y</code>都是实例对象<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">point</code>自身的属性（因为定义在<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">this</code>变量上），所以<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">hasOwnProperty</code>方法返回<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">true</code>，而<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">toString</code>是原型对象的属性（因为定义在<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">Point</code>类上），所以<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">hasOwnProperty</code>方法返回<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">false</code>。这些都与ES5的行为保持一致。</p><p style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin: 0px 0px 16px; padding: 0px; box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Roboto, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif, &quot;Apple Color Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Symbol&quot;;">与ES5一样，类的所有实例共享一个原型对象。</p><pre style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 16px; padding: 16px; box-sizing: border-box; font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-stretch: normal; font-size: 12px; line-height: 1.45; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; word-wrap: normal; overflow: auto; background-color: rgb(247, 247, 247); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51);"><code class="lang-javascript" style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0px; margin: 0px; background: 0px 0px transparent; border-radius: 3px; word-break: normal; white-space: pre; border: 0px; display: inline; overflow: visible; line-height: inherit; word-wrap: normal; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">var p1 = new Point(2,3);
var p2 = new Point(3,2);

p1.__proto__ === p2.__proto__
//true
</code></pre><p style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin: 0px 0px 16px; padding: 0px; box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Roboto, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif, &quot;Apple Color Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Symbol&quot;;">上面代码中，<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">p1</code>和<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">p2</code>都是Point的实例，它们的原型都是Point.prototype，所以<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">__proto__</code>属性是相等的。</p><p style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin: 0px 0px 16px; padding: 0px; box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Roboto, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif, &quot;Apple Color Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Symbol&quot;;">这也意味着，可以通过实例的<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">__proto__</code>属性为Class添加方法。</p><pre style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 16px; padding: 16px; box-sizing: border-box; font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-stretch: normal; font-size: 12px; line-height: 1.45; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; word-wrap: normal; overflow: auto; background-color: rgb(247, 247, 247); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51);"><code class="lang-javascript" style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0px; margin: 0px; background: 0px 0px transparent; border-radius: 3px; word-break: normal; white-space: pre; border: 0px; display: inline; overflow: visible; line-height: inherit; word-wrap: normal; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">var p1 = new Point(2,3);
var p2 = new Point(3,2);

p1.__proto__.printName = function () { return 'Oops' };

p1.printName() // "Oops"
p2.printName() // "Oops"

var p3 = new Point(4,2);
p3.printName() // "Oops"
</code></pre><p style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin: 0px 0px 16px; padding: 0px; box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Roboto, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif, &quot;Apple Color Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Symbol&quot;;">上面代码在<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">p1</code>的原型上添加了一个<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">printName</code>方法，由于<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">p1</code>的原型就是<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">p2</code>的原型，因此<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">p2</code>也可以调用这个方法。而且，此后新建的实例<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">p3</code>也可以调用这个方法。这意味着，使用实例的<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">__proto__</code>属性改写原型，必须相当谨慎，不推荐使用，因为这会改变Class的原始定义，影响到所有实例。</p><h3 id="-" style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin: 24px 0px 16px; padding: 0px; font-size: 1.25em; box-sizing: border-box; line-height: 1.25; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Roboto, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif, &quot;Apple Color Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Symbol&quot;;">不存在变量提升</h3><p style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin: 0px 0px 16px; padding: 0px; box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Roboto, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif, &quot;Apple Color Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Symbol&quot;;">Class不存在变量提升（hoist），这一点与ES5完全不同。</p><pre style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 16px; padding: 16px; box-sizing: border-box; font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-stretch: normal; font-size: 12px; line-height: 1.45; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; word-wrap: normal; overflow: auto; background-color: rgb(247, 247, 247); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51);"><code class="lang-javascript" style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0px; margin: 0px; background: 0px 0px transparent; border-radius: 3px; word-break: normal; white-space: pre; border: 0px; display: inline; overflow: visible; line-height: inherit; word-wrap: normal; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">new Foo(); // ReferenceError
class Foo {}
</code></pre><p style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin: 0px 0px 16px; padding: 0px; box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Roboto, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif, &quot;Apple Color Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Symbol&quot;;">上面代码中，<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">Foo</code>类使用在前，定义在后，这样会报错，因为ES6不会把类的声明提升到代码头部。这种规定的原因与下文要提到的继承有关，必须保证子类在父类之后定义。</p><pre style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 16px; padding: 16px; box-sizing: border-box; font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-stretch: normal; font-size: 12px; line-height: 1.45; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; word-wrap: normal; overflow: auto; background-color: rgb(247, 247, 247); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51);"><code class="lang-javascript" style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0px; margin: 0px; background: 0px 0px transparent; border-radius: 3px; word-break: normal; white-space: pre; border: 0px; display: inline; overflow: visible; line-height: inherit; word-wrap: normal; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">{
  let Foo = class {};
  class Bar extends Foo {
  }
}
</code></pre><p style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin: 0px 0px 16px; padding: 0px; box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Roboto, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif, &quot;Apple Color Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Symbol&quot;;">上面的代码不会报错，因为<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">Bar</code>继承<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">Foo</code>的时候，<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">Foo</code>已经有定义了。但是，如果存在<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">class</code>的提升，上面代码就会报错，因为<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">class</code>会被提升到代码头部，而<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">let</code>命令是不提升的，所以导致<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">Bar</code>继承<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">Foo</code>的时候，<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">Foo</code>还没有定义。</p><h3 id="class-" style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin: 24px 0px 16px; padding: 0px; font-size: 1.25em; box-sizing: border-box; line-height: 1.25; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Roboto, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif, &quot;Apple Color Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Symbol&quot;;">Class表达式</h3><p style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin: 0px 0px 16px; padding: 0px; box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Roboto, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif, &quot;Apple Color Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Symbol&quot;;">与函数一样，类也可以使用表达式的形式定义。</p><pre style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 16px; padding: 16px; box-sizing: border-box; font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-stretch: normal; font-size: 12px; line-height: 1.45; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; word-wrap: normal; overflow: auto; background-color: rgb(247, 247, 247); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51);"><code class="lang-javascript" style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0px; margin: 0px; background: 0px 0px transparent; border-radius: 3px; word-break: normal; white-space: pre; border: 0px; display: inline; overflow: visible; line-height: inherit; word-wrap: normal; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">const MyClass = class Me {
  getClassName() {
    return Me.name;
  }
};
</code></pre><p style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin: 0px 0px 16px; padding: 0px; box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Roboto, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif, &quot;Apple Color Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Symbol&quot;;">上面代码使用表达式定义了一个类。需要注意的是，这个类的名字是<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">MyClass</code>而不是<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">Me</code>，<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">Me</code>只在Class的内部代码可用，指代当前类。</p><pre style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 16px; padding: 16px; box-sizing: border-box; font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-stretch: normal; font-size: 12px; line-height: 1.45; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; word-wrap: normal; overflow: auto; background-color: rgb(247, 247, 247); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51);"><code class="lang-javascript" style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0px; margin: 0px; background: 0px 0px transparent; border-radius: 3px; word-break: normal; white-space: pre; border: 0px; display: inline; overflow: visible; line-height: inherit; word-wrap: normal; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">let inst = new MyClass();
inst.getClassName() // Me
Me.name // ReferenceError: Me is not defined
</code></pre><p style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin: 0px 0px 16px; padding: 0px; box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Roboto, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif, &quot;Apple Color Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Symbol&quot;;">上面代码表示，<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">Me</code>只在Class内部有定义。</p><p style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin: 0px 0px 16px; padding: 0px; box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Roboto, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif, &quot;Apple Color Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Symbol&quot;;">如果类的内部没用到的话，可以省略<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">Me</code>，也就是可以写成下面的形式。</p><pre style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 16px; padding: 16px; box-sizing: border-box; font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-stretch: normal; font-size: 12px; line-height: 1.45; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; word-wrap: normal; overflow: auto; background-color: rgb(247, 247, 247); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51);"><code class="lang-javascript" style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0px; margin: 0px; background: 0px 0px transparent; border-radius: 3px; word-break: normal; white-space: pre; border: 0px; display: inline; overflow: visible; line-height: inherit; word-wrap: normal; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">const MyClass = class { /* ... */ };
</code></pre><p style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin: 0px 0px 16px; padding: 0px; box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Roboto, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif, &quot;Apple Color Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Symbol&quot;;">采用Class表达式，可以写出立即执行的Class。</p><pre style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 16px; padding: 16px; box-sizing: border-box; font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-stretch: normal; font-size: 12px; line-height: 1.45; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; word-wrap: normal; overflow: auto; background-color: rgb(247, 247, 247); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51);"><code class="lang-javascript" style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0px; margin: 0px; background: 0px 0px transparent; border-radius: 3px; word-break: normal; white-space: pre; border: 0px; display: inline; overflow: visible; line-height: inherit; word-wrap: normal; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">let person = new class {
  constructor(name) {
    this.name = name;
  }

  sayName() {
    console.log(this.name);
  }
}('张三');

person.sayName(); // "张三"
</code></pre><p style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin: 0px 0px 16px; padding: 0px; box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Roboto, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif, &quot;Apple Color Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Symbol&quot;;">上面代码中，<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">person</code>是一个立即执行的类的实例。</p><h3 id="-" style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin: 24px 0px 16px; padding: 0px; font-size: 1.25em; box-sizing: border-box; line-height: 1.25; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Roboto, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif, &quot;Apple Color Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Symbol&quot;;">私有方法</h3><p style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin: 0px 0px 16px; padding: 0px; box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Roboto, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif, &quot;Apple Color Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Symbol&quot;;">私有方法是常见需求，但 ES6 不提供，只能通过变通方法模拟实现。</p><p style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin: 0px 0px 16px; padding: 0px; box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Roboto, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif, &quot;Apple Color Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Symbol&quot;;">一种做法是在命名上加以区别。</p><pre style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 16px; padding: 16px; box-sizing: border-box; font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-stretch: normal; font-size: 12px; line-height: 1.45; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; word-wrap: normal; overflow: auto; background-color: rgb(247, 247, 247); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51);"><code class="lang-javascript" style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0px; margin: 0px; background: 0px 0px transparent; border-radius: 3px; word-break: normal; white-space: pre; border: 0px; display: inline; overflow: visible; line-height: inherit; word-wrap: normal; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">class Widget {

  // 公有方法
  foo (baz) {
    this._bar(baz);
  }

  // 私有方法
  _bar(baz) {
    return this.snaf = baz;
  }

  // ...
}
</code></pre><p style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin: 0px 0px 16px; padding: 0px; box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Roboto, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif, &quot;Apple Color Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Symbol&quot;;">上面代码中，<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">_bar</code>方法前面的下划线，表示这是一个只限于内部使用的私有方法。但是，这种命名是不保险的，在类的外部，还是可以调用到这个方法。</p><p style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin: 0px 0px 16px; padding: 0px; box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Roboto, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif, &quot;Apple Color Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Symbol&quot;;">另一种方法就是索性将私有方法移出模块，因为模块内部的所有方法都是对外可见的。</p><pre style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 16px; padding: 16px; box-sizing: border-box; font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-stretch: normal; font-size: 12px; line-height: 1.45; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; word-wrap: normal; overflow: auto; background-color: rgb(247, 247, 247); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51);"><code class="lang-javascript" style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0px; margin: 0px; background: 0px 0px transparent; border-radius: 3px; word-break: normal; white-space: pre; border: 0px; display: inline; overflow: visible; line-height: inherit; word-wrap: normal; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">class Widget {
  foo (baz) {
    bar.call(this, baz);
  }

  // ...
}

function bar(baz) {
  return this.snaf = baz;
}
</code></pre><p style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin: 0px 0px 16px; padding: 0px; box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Roboto, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif, &quot;Apple Color Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Symbol&quot;;">上面代码中，<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">foo</code>是公有方法，内部调用了<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">bar.call(this, baz)</code>。这使得<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">bar</code>实际上成为了当前模块的私有方法。</p><p style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin: 0px 0px 16px; padding: 0px; box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Roboto, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif, &quot;Apple Color Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Symbol&quot;;">还有一种方法是利用<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">Symbol</code>值的唯一性，将私有方法的名字命名为一个<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">Symbol</code>值。</p><pre style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 16px; padding: 16px; box-sizing: border-box; font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-stretch: normal; font-size: 12px; line-height: 1.45; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; word-wrap: normal; overflow: auto; background-color: rgb(247, 247, 247); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51);"><code class="lang-javascript" style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0px; margin: 0px; background: 0px 0px transparent; border-radius: 3px; word-break: normal; white-space: pre; border: 0px; display: inline; overflow: visible; line-height: inherit; word-wrap: normal; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">const bar = Symbol('bar');
const snaf = Symbol('snaf');

export default class myClass{

  // 公有方法
  foo(baz) {
    this[bar](baz);
  }

  // 私有方法
  [bar](baz) {
    return this[snaf] = baz;
  }

  // ...
};
</code></pre><p style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin: 0px 0px 16px; padding: 0px; box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Roboto, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif, &quot;Apple Color Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Symbol&quot;;">上面代码中，<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">bar</code>和<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">snaf</code>都是<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px;
