-webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin: 0px 0px 16px; padding: 0px; box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Roboto, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif, &quot;Apple Color Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Symbol&quot;;">注意，<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">super</code>虽然代表了父类<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">A</code>的构造函数，但是返回的是子类<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">B</code>的实例，即<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">super</code>内部的<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">this</code>指的是<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">B</code>，因此<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">super()</code>在这里相当于<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">A.prototype.constructor.call(this)</code>。</p><pre style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 16px; padding: 16px; box-sizing: border-box; font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-stretch: normal; font-size: 12px; line-height: 1.45; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; word-wrap: normal; overflow: auto; background-color: rgb(247, 247, 247); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51);"><code class="lang-javascript" style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0px; margin: 0px; background: 0px 0px transparent; border-radius: 3px; word-break: normal; white-space: pre; border: 0px; display: inline; overflow: visible; line-height: inherit; word-wrap: normal; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">class A {
  constructor() {
    console.log(new.target.name);
  }
}
class B extends A {
  constructor() {
    super();
  }
}
new A() // A
new B() // B
</code></pre><p style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin: 0px 0px 16px; padding: 0px; box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Roboto, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif, &quot;Apple Color Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Symbol&quot;;">上面代码中，<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">new.target</code>指向当前正在执行的函数。可以看到，在<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">super()</code>执行时，它指向的是子类<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">B</code>的构造函数，而不是父类<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">A</code>的构造函数。也就是说，<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">super()</code>内部的<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">this</code>指向的是<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">B</code>。</p><p style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin: 0px 0px 16px; padding: 0px; box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Roboto, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif, &quot;Apple Color Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Symbol&quot;;">作为函数时，<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">super()</code>只能用在子类的构造函数之中，用在其他地方就会报错。</p><pre style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 16px; padding: 16px; box-sizing: border-box; font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-stretch: normal; font-size: 12px; line-height: 1.45; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; word-wrap: normal; overflow: auto; background-color: rgb(247, 247, 247); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51);"><code class="lang-javascript" style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0px; margin: 0px; background: 0px 0px transparent; border-radius: 3px; word-break: normal; white-space: pre; border: 0px; display: inline; overflow: visible; line-height: inherit; word-wrap: normal; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">class A {}

class B extends A {
  m() {
    super(); // 报错
  }
}
</code></pre><p style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin: 0px 0px 16px; padding: 0px; box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Roboto, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif, &quot;Apple Color Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Symbol&quot;;">上面代码中，<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">super()</code>用在<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">B</code>类的<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">m</code>方法之中，就会造成句法错误。</p><p style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin: 0px 0px 16px; padding: 0px; box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Roboto, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif, &quot;Apple Color Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Symbol&quot;;">第二种情况，<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">super</code>作为对象时，在普通方法中，指向父类的原型对象；在静态方法中，指向父类。</p><pre style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 16px; padding: 16px; box-sizing: border-box; font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-stretch: normal; font-size: 12px; line-height: 1.45; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; word-wrap: normal; overflow: auto; background-color: rgb(247, 247, 247); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51);"><code class="lang-javascript" style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0px; margin: 0px; background: 0px 0px transparent; border-radius: 3px; word-break: normal; white-space: pre; border: 0px; display: inline; overflow: visible; line-height: inherit; word-wrap: normal; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">class A {
  p() {
    return 2;
  }
}

class B extends A {
  constructor() {
    super();
    console.log(super.p()); // 2
  }
}

let b = new B();
</code></pre><p style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin: 0px 0px 16px; padding: 0px; box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Roboto, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif, &quot;Apple Color Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Symbol&quot;;">上面代码中，子类<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">B</code>当中的<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">super.p()</code>，就是将<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">super</code>当作一个对象使用。这时，<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">super</code>在普通方法之中，指向<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">A.prototype</code>，所以<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">super.p()</code>就相当于<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">A.prototype.p()</code>。</p><p style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin: 0px 0px 16px; padding: 0px; box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Roboto, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif, &quot;Apple Color Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Symbol&quot;;">这里需要注意，由于<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">super</code>指向父类的原型对象，所以定义在父类实例上的方法或属性，是无法通过<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">super</code>调用的。</p><pre style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 16px; padding: 16px; box-sizing: border-box; font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-stretch: normal; font-size: 12px; line-height: 1.45; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; word-wrap: normal; overflow: auto; background-color: rgb(247, 247, 247); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51);"><code class="lang-javascript" style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0px; margin: 0px; background: 0px 0px transparent; border-radius: 3px; word-break: normal; white-space: pre; border: 0px; display: inline; overflow: visible; line-height: inherit; word-wrap: normal; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">class A {
  constructor() {
    this.p = 2;
  }
}

class B extends A {
  get m() {
    return super.p;
  }
}

let b = new B();
b.m // undefined
</code></pre><p style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin: 0px 0px 16px; padding: 0px; box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Roboto, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif, &quot;Apple Color Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Symbol&quot;;">上面代码中，<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">p</code>是父类<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">A</code>实例的属性，<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">super.p</code>就引用不到它。</p><p style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin: 0px 0px 16px; padding: 0px; box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Roboto, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif, &quot;Apple Color Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Symbol&quot;;">如果属性定义在父类的原型对象上，<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">super</code>就可以取到。</p><pre style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 16px; padding: 16px; box-sizing: border-box; font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-stretch: normal; font-size: 12px; line-height: 1.45; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; word-wrap: normal; overflow: auto; background-color: rgb(247, 247, 247); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51);"><code class="lang-javascript" style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0px; margin: 0px; background: 0px 0px transparent; border-radius: 3px; word-break: normal; white-space: pre; border: 0px; display: inline; overflow: visible; line-height: inherit; word-wrap: normal; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">class A {}
A.prototype.x = 2;

class B extends A {
  constructor() {
    super();
    console.log(super.x) // 2
  }
}

let b = new B();
</code></pre><p style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin: 0px 0px 16px; padding: 0px; box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Roboto, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif, &quot;Apple Color Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Symbol&quot;;">上面代码中，属性<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">x</code>是定义在<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">A.prototype</code>上面的，所以<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">super.x</code>可以取到它的值。</p><p style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin: 0px 0px 16px; padding: 0px; box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Roboto, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif, &quot;Apple Color Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Symbol&quot;;">ES6 规定，通过<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">super</code>调用父类的方法时，<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">super</code>会绑定子类的<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">this</code>。</p><pre style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 16px; padding: 16px; box-sizing: border-box; font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-stretch: normal; font-size: 12px; line-height: 1.45; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; word-wrap: normal; overflow: auto; background-color: rgb(247, 247, 247); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51);"><code class="lang-javascript" style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0px; margin: 0px; background: 0px 0px transparent; border-radius: 3px; word-break: normal; white-space: pre; border: 0px; display: inline; overflow: visible; line-height: inherit; word-wrap: normal; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">class A {
  constructor() {
    this.x = 1;
  }
  print() {
    console.log(this.x);
  }
}

class B extends A {
  constructor() {
    super();
    this.x = 2;
  }
  m() {
    super.print();
  }
}

let b = new B();
b.m() // 2
</code></pre><p style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin: 0px 0px 16px; padding: 0px; box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Roboto, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif, &quot;Apple Color Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Symbol&quot;;">上面代码中，<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">super.print()</code>虽然调用的是<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">A.prototype.print()</code>，但是<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">A.prototype.print()</code>会绑定子类<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">B</code>的<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">this</code>，导致输出的是<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">2</code>，而不是<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">1</code>。也就是说，实际上执行的是<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">super.print.call(this)</code>。</p><p style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin: 0px 0px 16px; padding: 0px; box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Roboto, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif, &quot;Apple Color Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Symbol&quot;;">由于绑定子类的<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">this</code>，所以如果通过<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">super</code>对某个属性赋值，这时<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">super</code>就是<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">this</code>，赋值的属性会变成子类实例的属性。</p><pre style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 16px; padding: 16px; box-sizing: border-box; font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-stretch: normal; font-size: 12px; line-height: 1.45; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; word-wrap: normal; overflow: auto; background-color: rgb(247, 247, 247); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51);"><code class="lang-javascript" style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0px; margin: 0px; background: 0px 0px transparent; border-radius: 3px; word-break: normal; white-space: pre; border: 0px; display: inline; overflow: visible; line-height: inherit; word-wrap: normal; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">class A {
  constructor() {
    this.x = 1;
  }
}

class B extends A {
  constructor() {
    super();
    this.x = 2;
    super.x = 3;
    console.log(super.x); // undefined
    console.log(this.x); // 3
  }
}

let b = new B();
</code></pre><p style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin: 0px 0px 16px; padding: 0px; box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Roboto, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif, &quot;Apple Color Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Symbol&quot;;">上面代码中，<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">super.x</code>赋值为<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">3</code>，这时等同于对<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">this.x</code>赋值为<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">3</code>。而当读取<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">super.x</code>的时候，读的是<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">A.prototype.x</code>，所以返回<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">undefined</code>。</p><p style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin: 0px 0px 16px; padding: 0px; box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Roboto, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif, &quot;Apple Color Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Symbol&quot;;">如果<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">super</code>作为对象，用在静态方法之中，这时<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">super</code>将指向父类，而不是父类的原型对象。</p><pre style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 16px; padding: 16px; box-sizing: border-box; font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-stretch: normal; font-size: 12px; line-height: 1.45; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; word-wrap: normal; overflow: auto; background-color: rgb(247, 247, 247); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51);"><code class="lang-javascript" style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0px; margin: 0px; background: 0px 0px transparent; border-radius: 3px; word-break: normal; white-space: pre; border: 0px; display: inline; overflow: visible; line-height: inherit; word-wrap: normal; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">class Parent {
  static myMethod(msg) {
    console.log('static', msg);
  }

  myMethod(msg) {
    console.log('instance', msg);
  }
}

class Child extends Parent {
  static myMethod(msg) {
    super.myMethod(msg);
  }

  myMethod(msg) {
    super.myMethod(msg);
  }
}

Child.myMethod(1); // static 1

var child = new Child();
child.myMethod(2); // instance 2
</code></pre><p style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin: 0px 0px 16px; padding: 0px; box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Roboto, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif, &quot;Apple Color Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Symbol&quot;;">上面代码中，<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">super</code>在静态方法之中指向父类，在普通方法之中指向父类的原型对象。</p><p style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin: 0px 0px 16px; padding: 0px; box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Roboto, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif, &quot;Apple Color Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Symbol&quot;;">注意，使用<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">super</code>的时候，必须显式指定是作为函数、还是作为对象使用，否则会报错。</p><pre style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 16px; padding: 16px; box-sizing: border-box; font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-stretch: normal; font-size: 12px; line-height: 1.45; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; word-wrap: normal; overflow: auto; background-color: rgb(247, 247, 247); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51);"><code class="lang-javascript" style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0px; margin: 0px; background: 0px 0px transparent; border-radius: 3px; word-break: normal; white-space: pre; border: 0px; display: inline; overflow: visible; line-height: inherit; word-wrap: normal; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">class A {}

class B extends A {
  constructor() {
    super();
    console.log(super); // 报错
  }
}
</code></pre><p style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin: 0px 0px 16px; padding: 0px; box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Roboto, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif, &quot;Apple Color Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Symbol&quot;;">上面代码中，<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">console.log(super)</code>当中的<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">super</code>，无法看出是作为函数使用，还是作为对象使用，所以 JavaScript 引擎解析代码的时候就会报错。这时，如果能清晰地表明<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">super</code>的数据类型，就不会报错。</p><pre style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 16px; padding: 16px; box-sizing: border-box; font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-stretch: normal; font-size: 12px; line-height: 1.45; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; word-wrap: normal; overflow: auto; background-color: rgb(247, 247, 247); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51);"><code class="lang-javascript" style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0px; margin: 0px; background: 0px 0px transparent; border-radius: 3px; word-break: normal; white-space: pre; border: 0px; display: inline; overflow: visible; line-height: inherit; word-wrap: normal; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">class A {}

class B extends A {
  constructor() {
    super();
    console.log(super.valueOf() instanceof B); // true
  }
}

let b = new B();
</code></pre><p style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin: 0px 0px 16px; padding: 0px; box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Roboto, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif, &quot;Apple Color Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Symbol&quot;;">上面代码中，<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">super.valueOf()</code>表明<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">super</code>是一个对象，因此就不会报错。同时，由于<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">super</code>绑定<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">B</code>的<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">this</code>，所以<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">super.valueOf()</code>返回的是一个<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">B</code>的实例。</p><p style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin: 0px 0px 16px; padding: 0px; box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Roboto, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif, &quot;Apple Color Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Symbol&quot;;">最后，由于对象总是继承其他对象的，所以可以在任意一个对象中，使用<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">super</code>关键字。</p><pre style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 16px; padding: 16px; box-sizing: border-box; font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-stretch: normal; font-size: 12px; line-height: 1.45; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; word-wrap: normal; overflow: auto; background-color: rgb(247, 247, 247); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51);"><code class="lang-javascript" style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0px; margin: 0px; background: 0px 0px transparent; border-radius: 3px; word-break: normal; white-space: pre; border: 0px; display: inline; overflow: visible; line-height: inherit; word-wrap: normal; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">var obj = {
  toString() {
    return "MyObject: " + super.toString();
  }
};

obj.toString(); // MyObject: [object Object]
</code></pre><h3 id="-_-_proto-_-_-" style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin: 24px 0px 16px; padding: 0px; font-size: 1.25em; box-sizing: border-box; line-height: 1.25; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Roboto, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif, &quot;Apple Color Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Symbol&quot;;">实例的__proto__属性</h3><p style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin: 0px 0px 16px; padding: 0px; box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Roboto, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif, &quot;Apple Color Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Symbol&quot;;">子类实例的__proto__属性的__proto__属性，指向父类实例的__proto__属性。也就是说，子类的原型的原型，是父类的原型。</p><pre style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 16px; padding: 16px; box-sizing: border-box; font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-stretch: normal; font-size: 12px; line-height: 1.45; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; word-wrap: normal; overflow: auto; background-color: rgb(247, 247, 247); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51);"><code class="lang-javascript" style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0px; margin: 0px; background: 0px 0px transparent; border-radius: 3px; word-break: normal; white-space: pre; border: 0px; display: inline; overflow: visible; line-height: inherit; word-wrap: normal; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">var p1 = new Point(2, 3);
var p2 = new ColorPoint(2, 3, 'red');

p2.__proto__ === p1.__proto__ // false
p2.__proto__.__proto__ === p1.__proto__ // true
</code></pre><p style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin: 0px 0px 16px; padding: 0px; box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Roboto, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif, &quot;Apple Color Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Symbol&quot;;">上面代码中，<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">ColorPoint</code>继承了<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">Point</code>，导致前者原型的原型是后者的原型。</p><p style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin: 0px 0px 16px; padding: 0px; box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Roboto, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif, &quot;Apple Color Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Symbol&quot;;">因此，通过子类实例的<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">__proto__.__proto__</code>属性，可以修改父类实例的行为。</p><pre style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 16px; padding: 16px; box-sizing: border-box; font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-stretch: normal; font-size: 12px; line-height: 1.45; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; word-wrap: normal; overflow: auto; background-color: rgb(247, 247, 247); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51);"><code class="lang-javascript" style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0px; margin: 0px; background: 0px 0px transparent; border-radius: 3px; word-break: normal; white-space: pre; border: 0px; display: inline; overflow: visible; line-height: inherit; word-wrap: normal; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">p2.__proto__.__proto__.printName = function () {
  console.log('Ha');
};

p1.printName() // "Ha"
</code></pre><p style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin: 0px 0px 16px; padding: 0px; box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Roboto, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif, &quot;Apple Color Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Symbol&quot;;">上面代码在<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">ColorPoint</code>的实例<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">p2</code>上向<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">Point</code>类添加方法，结果影响到了<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">Point</code>的实例<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">p1</code>。</p><h2 id="-" style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin: 24px 0px 16px; padding: 0px 0px 0.3em; top: -900em; left: -900em; box-sizing: border-box; border-bottom: 1px solid rgb(238, 238, 238); line-height: 1.25; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Roboto, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif, &quot;Apple Color Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Symbol&quot;;">原生构造函数的继承</h2><p style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin: 0px 0px 16px; padding: 0px; box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Roboto, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif, &quot;Apple Color Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Symbol&quot;;">原生构造函数是指语言内置的构造函数，通常用来生成数据结构。ECMAScript的原生构造函数大致有下面这些。</p><ul style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin: 0px 0px 16px; padding: 0px 0px 0px 2em; list-style: none; box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Roboto, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif, &quot;Apple Color Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Symbol&quot;;"><li style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin: 0px; padding: 0px; box-sizing: border-box;">Boolean()</li><li style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin: 0.25em 0px 0px; padding: 0px; box-sizing: border-box;">Number()</li><li style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin: 0.25em 0px 0px; padding: 0px; box-sizing: border-box;">String()</li><li style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin: 0.25em 0px 0px; padding: 0px; box-sizing: border-box;">Array()</li><li style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin: 0.25em 0px 0px; padding: 0px; box-sizing: border-box;">Date()</li><li style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin: 0.25em 0px 0px; padding: 0px; box-sizing: border-box;">Function()</li><li style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin: 0.25em 0px 0px; padding: 0px; box-sizing: border-box;">RegExp()</li><li style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin: 0.25em 0px 0px; padding: 0px; box-sizing: border-box;">Error()</li><li style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin: 0.25em 0px 0px; padding: 0px; box-sizing: border-box;">Object()</li></ul><p style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin: 0px 0px 16px; padding: 0px; box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Roboto, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif, &quot;Apple Color Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Symbol&quot;;">以前，这些原生构造函数是无法继承的，比如，不能自己定义一个<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">Array</code>的子类。</p><pre style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 16px; padding: 16px; box-sizing: border-box; font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-stretch: normal; font-size: 12px; line-height: 1.45; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; word-wrap: normal; overflow: auto; background-color: rgb(247, 247, 247); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51);"><code class="lang-javascript" style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0px; margin: 0px; background: 0px 0px transparent; border-radius: 3px; word-break: normal; white-space: pre; border: 0px; display: inline; overflow: visible; line-height: inherit; word-wrap: normal; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">function MyArray() {
  Array.apply(this, arguments);
}

MyArray.prototype = Object.create(Array.prototype, {
  constructor: {
    value: MyArray,
    writable: true,
    configurable: true,
    enumerable: true
  }
});
</code></pre><p style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin: 0px 0px 16px; padding: 0px; box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Roboto, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif, &quot;Apple Color Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Symbol&quot;;">上面代码定义了一个继承Array的<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">MyArray</code>类。但是，这个类的行为与<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">Array</code>完全不一致。</p><pre style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 16px; padding: 16px; box-sizing: border-box; font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-stretch: normal; font-size: 12px; line-height: 1.45; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; word-wrap: normal; overflow: auto; background-color: rgb(247, 247, 247); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51);"><code class="lang-javascript" style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0px; margin: 0px; background: 0px 0px transparent; border-radius: 3px; word-break: normal; white-space: pre; border: 0px; display: inline; overflow: visible; line-height: inherit; word-wrap: normal; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">var colors = new MyArray();
colors[0] = "red";
colors.length  // 0

colors.length = 0;
colors[0]  // "red"
</code></pre><p style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin: 0px 0px 16px; padding: 0px; box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Roboto, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif, &quot;Apple Color Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Symbol&quot;;">之所以会发生这种情况，是因为子类无法获得原生构造函数的内部属性，通过<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">Array.apply()</code>或者分配给原型对象都不行。原生构造函数会忽略<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">apply</code>方法传入的<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">this</code>，也就是说，原生构造函数的<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">this</code>无法绑定，导致拿不到内部属性。</p><p style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin: 0px 0px 16px; padding: 0px; box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Roboto, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif, &quot;Apple Color Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Symbol&quot;;">ES5是先新建子类的实例对象<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">this</code>，再将父类的属性添加到子类上，由于父类的内部属性无法获取，导致无法继承原生的构造函数。比如，Array构造函数有一个内部属性<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">[[DefineOwnProperty]]</code>，用来定义新属性时，更新<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">length</code>属性，这个内部属性无法在子类获取，导致子类的<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">length</code>属性行为不正常。</p><p style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin: 0px 0px 16px; padding: 0px; box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Roboto, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif, &quot;Apple Color Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Symbol&quot;;">下面的例子中，我们想让一个普通对象继承<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">Error</code>对象。</p><pre style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 16px; padding: 16px; box-sizing: border-box; font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-stretch: normal; font-size: 12px; line-height: 1.45; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; word-wrap: normal; overflow: auto; background-color: rgb(247, 247, 247); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51);"><code class="lang-javascript" style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0px; margin: 0px; background: 0px 0px transparent; border-radius: 3px; word-break: normal; white-space: pre; border: 0px; display: inline; overflow: visible; line-height: inherit; word-wrap: normal; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">var e = {};

Object.getOwnPropertyNames(Error.call(e))
// [ 'stack' ]

Object.getOwnPropertyNames(e)
// []
</code></pre><p style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin: 0px 0px 16px; padding: 0px; box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Roboto, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif, &quot;Apple Color Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Symbol&quot;;">上面代码中，我们想通过<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">Error.call(e)</code>这种写法，让普通对象<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">e</code>具有<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">Error</code>对象的实例属性。但是，<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">Error.call()</code>完全忽略传入的第一个参数，而是返回一个新对象，<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">e</code>本身没有任何变化。这证明了<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">Error.call(e)</code>这种写法，无法继承原生构造函数。</p><p style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin: 0px 0px 16px; padding: 0px; box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Roboto, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif, &quot;Apple Color Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Symbol&quot;;">ES6允许继承原生构造函数定义子类，因为ES6是先新建父类的实例对象<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">this</code>，然后再用子类的构造函数修饰<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">this</code>，使得父类的所有行为都可以继承。下面是一个继承<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">Array</code>的例子。</p><pre style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 16px; padding: 16px; box-sizing: border-box; font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-stretch: normal; font-size: 12px; line-height: 1.45; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; word-wrap: normal; overflow: auto; background-color: rgb(247, 247, 247); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51);"><code class="lang-javascript" style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0px; margin: 0px; background: 0px 0px transparent; border-radius: 3px; word-break: normal; white-space: pre; border: 0px; display: inline; overflow: visible; line-height: inherit; word-wrap: normal; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">class MyArray extends Array {
  constructor(...args) {
    super(...args);
  }
}

var arr = new MyArray();
arr[0] = 12;
arr.length // 1

arr.length = 0;
arr[0] // undefined
</code></pre><p style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin: 0px 0px 16px; padding: 0px; box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Roboto, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif, &quot;Apple Color Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Symbol&quot;;">上面代码定义了一个<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">MyArray</code>类，继承了<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">Array</code>构造函数，因此就可以从<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">MyArray</code>生成数组的实例。这意味着，ES6可以自定义原生数据结构（比如Array、String等）的子类，这是ES5无法做到的。</p><p style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin: 0px 0px 16px; padding: 0px; box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Roboto, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif, &quot;Apple Color Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Symbol&quot;;">上面这个例子也说明，<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">extends</code>关键字不仅可以用来继承类，还可以用来继承原生的构造函数。因此可以在原生数据结构的基础上，定义自己的数据结构。下面就是定义了一个带版本功能的数组。</p><pre style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 16px; padding: 16px; box-sizing: border-box; font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-stretch: normal; font-size: 12px; line-height: 1.45; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; word-wrap: normal; overflow: auto; background-color: rgb(247, 247, 247); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51);"><code class="lang-javascript" style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0px; margin: 0px; background: 0px 0px transparent; border-radius: 3px; word-break: normal; white-space: pre; border: 0px; display: inline; overflow: visible; line-height: inherit; word-wrap: normal; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">class VersionedArray extends Array {
  constructor() {
    super();
    this.history = [[]];
  }
  commit() {
    this.history.push(this.slice());
  }
  revert() {
    this.splice(0, this.length, ...this.history[this.history.length - 1]);
  }
}

var x = new VersionedArray();

x.push(1);
x.push(2);
x // [1, 2]
x.history // [[]]

x.commit();
x.history // [[], [1, 2]]
x.push(3);
x // [1, 2, 3]

x.revert();
x // [1, 2]
</code></pre><p style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin: 0px 0px 16px; padding: 0px; box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Roboto, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif, &quot;Apple Color Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Symbol&quot;;">上面代码中，<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">VersionedArray</code>结构会通过<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">commit</code>方法，将自己的当前状态存入<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">history</code>属性，然后通过<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">revert</code>方法，可以撤销当前版本，回到上一个版本。除此之外，<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">VersionedArray</code>依然是一个数组，所有原生的数组方法都可以在它上面调用。</p><p style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin: 0px 0px 16px; padding: 0px; box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Roboto, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif, &quot;Apple Color Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Symbol&quot;;">下面是一个自定义<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">Error</code>子类的例子。</p><pre style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 16px; padding: 16px; box-sizing: border-box; font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-stretch: normal; font-size: 12px; line-height: 1.45; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; word-wrap: normal; overflow: auto; background-color: rgb(247, 247, 247); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51);"><code class="lang-javascript" style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0px; margin: 0px; background: 0px 0px transparent; border-radius: 3px; word-break: normal; white-space: pre; border: 0px; display: inline; overflow: visible; line-height: inherit; word-wrap: normal; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">class ExtendableError extends Error {
  constructor(message) {
    super();
    this.message = message;
    this.stack = (new Error()).stack;
    this.name = this.constructor.name;
  }
}

class MyError extends ExtendableError {
  constructor(m) {
    super(m);
  }
}

var myerror = new MyError('ll');
myerror.message // "ll"
myerror instanceof Error // true
myerror.name // "MyError"
myerror.stack
// Error
//     at MyError.ExtendableError
//     ...
</code></pre><p style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin: 0px 0px 16px; padding: 0px; box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Roboto, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif, &quot;Apple Color Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Symbol&quot;;">注意，继承<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">Object</code>的子类，有一个<a href="http://stackoverflow.com/questions/36203614/super-does-not-pass-arguments-when-instantiating-a-class-extended-from-object" style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; outline: 0px; color: rgb(64, 120, 192); text-decoration-line: none; box-sizing: border-box; background-color: transparent;">行为差异</a>。</p><pre style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 16px; padding: 16px; box-sizing: border-box; font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-stretch: normal; font-size: 12px; line-height: 1.45; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; word-wrap: normal; overflow: auto; background-color: rgb(247, 247, 247); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51);"><code class="lang-javascript" style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0px; margin: 0px; background: 0px 0px transparent; border-radius: 3px; word-break: normal; white-space: pre; border: 0px; display: inline; overflow: visible; line-height: inherit; word-wrap: normal; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">class NewObj extends Object{
  constructor(){
    super(...arguments);
  }
}
var o = new NewObj({attr: true});
console.log(o.attr === true);  // false
</code></pre><p style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin: 0px 0px 16px; padding: 0px; box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Roboto, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif, &quot;Apple Color Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Symbol&quot;;">上面代码中，<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04);
